Diagnosis of this disease is made by following blood tests:  CBC, Blood Lipid Profile, Serum Ferritin, Serum GGT, Serum Alkaline Phosphatase, Liver Function Test, and Lipid Profile. Treatment of this disease includes:  Lifestyle modification, Nutritional counsel

  True Answer: concussion
  Predicted: concussion 

A concussion is a head injury that disrupts your brain function. Symptoms of a concussion can include dizziness, double vision, vomiting, and difficulty speaking. Other symptoms may include headache, loss of sensation, nausea, and rib pain. A person with a concussion may also experience blurred vision, seizures, and changes in emotional state. It is important to seek medical attention if you have any of these symptoms. Diagnosis is made after a thorough medical evaluation, including a head injury history and a ne

The correct answer is liver disease. The symptoms of this condition include abdominal pain, nausea, side pain, and back pain. A liver disease may also cause symptoms such as jaundice, itching, and feeling sick.  Diagnosis is made by a physician based on the medical history, a physical examination, and the results of tests such as blood tests, imaging studies, and liver function tests.

[1035] ✗ WRONG
  Question: I have these symptoms: blood in urine, frequent urination, side pain, back pain, painful urination, and lower abdominal pain. What do I have?
  True Answer: cystitis
  Predicted: kidney stone.

A kidney stone is a hard mass that can form in the kidneys and obstruct the flow of urine. The symptoms of a kidney stone can include side pain, back pain, and blood in the urine. Myositis is a condition that causes muscle weakness and fatigue, and may also cause side pain. Myositis is not typically associated with kidney stones.

This is a very common condition.  It can be caused by bacteria, viruses, and parasites.  Common bacterial causes are streptococcus, staphylococcus, and pneumococcus.  Common viral causes are respiratory syncytial virus (RSV), influenza, and pertussis.  Common parasitic causes are toxoplasmosis, malaria, and strongyloidiasis.

[1902] ✗ WRONG
  Question: My symptoms are irregular appearing scalp, skin moles, warts, itching of skin, skin irritation, abnormal appearing skin, and skin swelling. What could this be?
  True Answer: seborrheic keratosis
  Predicted: skin polyp

This is a skin growth. It could be a skin tag, skin cancer, or a skin polyp. Skin polyps are benign growths that develop in the skin and are usually found on sun exposed areas of the body. They are usually painless and do not require treatment. However, if the skin polyp becomes irritated or infected, it may need to be removed. A skin polyp may also be mistaken for a cancerous growth. A skin biopsy is needed to confirm the diagnosis.
